			limit = {
				owner.ideology_traditionalist_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = { # Uses 17 rather than 12, because caste system doesn't count by default

				multiply = 17
			}

				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}

		}

			add = 50
		}

			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_character = {
						has_template = RUS_alexander_iii
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# Women won't favor highly patriarchal ideologies
		if = {
			limit = {
				leader = {
					is_female = yes
				}
			}
			multiply = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}

		law_dirigisme = disapprove
		law_command_cooperative_economy = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_language_policy = {
		law_local_vernacular = neutral
		law_civic_monolingualism = neutral
		law_multilingual_federalism = strongly_approve
		law_linguistic_purity = strongly_disapprove

		law_ministry_of_refugee_affairs = approve
	}
	lawgroup_ministry_of_intelligence_and_security = {
		law_no_ministry_of_intelligence_and_security = approve
		law_ministry_of_intelligence_and_security = neutral
	}
	lawgroup_criminal_justice = {
		law_punishment_focused_criminal_justice = disapprove
		law_rehabilitation_focused_criminal_justice = strongly_approve
		law_restorative_justice = neutral
	}
	lawgroup_LGBTQ_rights = {
		law_active_persecution = strongly_disapprove
		law_legal_limbo = disapprove
		law_basic_protections = neutral
		law_comprehensive_rights = approve
		law_full_equality_and_protection = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_privacy_rights = {
		law_minimal_privacy_protection = neutral
		law_moderate_data_privacy = approve
		law_strong_privacy_rights = strongly_approve
		law_intrusive_surveillance = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_governance_principles = {
		law_direct_democracy = strongly_approve
		law_corporation_state = disapprove # If these stances are changed, update ideology_radical_favoured_laws and ideology_radical_disfavoured_laws.
		law_monarchy = strongly_disapprove
		law_theocracy = strongly_disapprove
		law_council_republic = strongly_disapprove
		law_presidential_republic = neutral
		law_parliamentary_republic = approve
		law_corporate_state = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_distribution_of_power = {
		law_algorithmic_governance = disapprove
		law_universal_suffrage = strongly_approve
		law_census_voting = approve
		law_wealth_voting = neutral
		law_technocracy = disapprove
		law_landed_voting = disapprove
		law_anarchy = strongly_disapprove
		law_oligarchy = strongly_disapprove
		law_autocracy = strongly_disapprove
		law_single_party_state = disapprove

	lawgroup_free_speech = {
		law_protected_speech = strongly_approve
		law_right_of_assembly = approve
		law_censorship = disapprove
		law_outlawed_dissent = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_internal_security = {
		law_guaranteed_liberties = strongly_approve
		law_no_home_affairs = neutral

		law_public_schools = approve
		law_private_schools = neutral
		law_no_schools = disapprove
		law_religious_schools = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_labour_associations = { # The Sans-Culottes resented the ban on workers' associations.
		law_combination_acts = disapprove
		law_guild_system = strongly_disapprove
		law_anti_strike_laws = neutral
		law_corporatized_unions = disapprove
		law_right_to_associate = neutral
		law_factory_councils = strongly_disapprove
	}
	country_trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = egalitarianism
		# Invalid for pre-ACW USA whilst Jacksonian Democrats are relevant
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				exists = c:USA
				OR = {
					c:USA = this
					civil_war_origin_country ?= c:USA
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_journal_entry = je_acw_countdown
				any_scope_character = {
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_jacksonian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_radical_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		# Agitators should have an ideology at odds with current laws
		NAND = {
			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
				}
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_protected_speech
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_guaranteed_liberties
			}
		}
		# Monarchs cannot be republicans
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
			OR = {
				is_ruler = yes
				is_heir = yes
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_radical_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if people are angry
		add = {
			value = owner.radical_fraction
			multiply = 100
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_radical_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_radical_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 9
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_radical_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_radical_favoured_laws
				multiply = 9
			}
		}
		# Labour Association Laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						has_technology_researched = socialism
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_combination_acts
					}
				}
				add = 50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						OR = {
							has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_guild_system
							has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anti_strike_laws
						}
					}
				}
				add = 25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_right_to_associate
					}
				}
				add = -25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
					}
				}
				add = -50
			}
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Hungarian Revolution was successful.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hungarian_revolution_increased_liberalism
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Pedro JE victory
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = brz_enduring_empire
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
					OR = {
						capital.region = sr:region_north_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_south_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_england
						capital.region = sr:region_iberia
						capital.region = sr:region_france
						capital.region = sr:region_occitania
						capital.region = sr:region_rhine
						capital.region = sr:region_italy
						capital.region = sr:region_poland
						capital.region = sr:region_danubia
						capital.region = sr:region_balkans
						capital.region = sr:region_baltic
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = {
				value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = post_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = counter_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 0.5 }
		}
		# Becomes less prevalent after socialism is researched
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology_researched = socialism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				}
				multiply = 0.05
			}
			else = {
				multiply = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if people are angry
		add = {
			value = owner.radical_fraction
			multiply = 100
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_radical_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_radical_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 9
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_radical_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_radical_favoured_laws
				multiply = 9
			}
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				has_variable = spa_liberal_military_var
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Labour Association Laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						has_technology_researched = socialism
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_combination_acts
					}
				}
				add = 50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						OR = {
							has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_guild_system
							has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anti_strike_laws
						}
					}
				}
				add = 25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_right_to_associate
					}
				}
				add = -25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					owner = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
					}
				}
				add = -50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
					OR = {
						capital.region = sr:region_north_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_south_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_england
						capital.region = sr:region_iberia
						capital.region = sr:region_france
						capital.region = sr:region_occitania
						capital.region = sr:region_rhine
						capital.region = sr:region_italy
						capital.region = sr:region_poland
						capital.region = sr:region_danubia
						capital.region = sr:region_balkans
						capital.region = sr:region_baltic
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = {
				value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = post_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = counter_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 0.5 }
		}
		# Becomes less prevalent after socialism is researched
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology_researched = socialism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					interest_group = {
						is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					}
				}
				multiply = 0.05
			}
			else = {
				multiply = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

				}

			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				ig_approval >= 0
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Hungarian Revolution was successful.

			add = 50

				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# extremely unlikely for trade unions in council republic
		if = {

				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions

					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.01
		}
		# National Liberation Alliance
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = national_liberation_alliance_variable
					has_journal_entry = je_new_republic
				}
			}
			multiply = 1.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_social_democrat_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_social_democrat_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 10 # Caste laws don't count by default
			}
		}
		# very angry IG's more likely to turn to more radical socialism
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_interest_group_type = ig_devout } # can't be radical socialists
				interest_group.ig_approval <= -5
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# more likely for content devout in council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
				interest_group.ig_approval >= 0
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# more likely for content trade unions outside of council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				interest_group.ig_approval >= 0
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				has_variable = spa_liberal_military_var
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# extremely unlikely for trade unions in council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.01
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

		law_freedom_of_information = disapprove
		law_open_government = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_rules_of_war = {
		law_traditional_rules_of_war = approve
		law_war_crimes_forbidden = neutral
		law_humanitarian_regulations = disapprove
		law_limited_war = strongly_disapprove
		law_total_war = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_LGBTQ_rights = {
		law_active_persecution = strongly_approve
		law_legal_limbo = approve
		law_basic_protections = neutral
		law_comprehensive_rights = disapprove
		law_full_equality_and_protection = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_human_augmentation = {
		law_no_augmentation = neutral
		law_unrestricted_augmentation = strongly_disapprove
		law_human_purity = strongly_approve
		law_medical_augmentation_only = strongly_disapprove
		law_regulated_augmentation_market = strongly_disapprove
		law_mandatory_augmentation = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_privacy_rights = {
		law_minimal_privacy_protection = strongly_disapprove
		law_moderate_data_privacy = strongly_disapprove
		law_strong_privacy_rights = strongly_disapprove
		law_intrusive_surveillance = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_distribution_of_power = {
		law_algorithmic_governance = disapprove
		law_single_party_state = strongly_approve
		law_autocracy = approve
		law_oligarchy = neutral
		law_technocracy = neutral
		law_anarchy = strongly_disapprove
		law_universal_suffrage = disapprove
		law_census_voting = disapprove
		law_wealth_voting = disapprove
		law_landed_voting = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_citizenship = {
		law_ethnostate = strongly_approve
		law_national_supremacy = approve
		law_subjecthood = strongly_disapprove
		law_racial_segregation = approve
		law_cultural_exclusion = disapprove
		law_multicultural = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_army_model = {
		law_mass_conscription = strongly_approve
		law_professional_army = approve
		law_national_militia = disapprove
		law_peasant_levies = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_free_speech = {
		law_protected_speech = strongly_disapprove
		law_right_of_assembly = disapprove
		law_censorship = neutral
		law_outlawed_dissent = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_governance_principles = {
		law_theocracy = disapprove
		law_monarchy = neutral
		law_presidential_republic = neutral
		law_parliamentary_republic = neutral
		law_corporate_state = approve
		law_council_republic = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_labour_associations = {
		law_combination_acts = neutral
		law_guild_system = approve
		law_anti_strike_laws = approve
		law_corporatized_unions = strongly_approve
		law_right_to_associate = disapprove
		law_factory_councils = strongly_disapprove
	}
	country_trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = political_agitation
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_fascist_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		# Agitator ideologies should disapprove of a current law
		NAND = {
			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_ethnostate
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_outlawed_dissent
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_militarized_police
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_fascist_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# More likely if people are angry
		add = {
			value = owner.radical_fraction
			multiply = 100
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_fascist_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_fascist_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_fascist_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_fascist_favoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# More likely if paying war reparations
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					any_scope_treaty = {
						is_enforced = yes
						any_scope_article = {
							has_type = money_transfer
							source_country = root.owner
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# More likely with a convenient scapegoat
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_incorporated = yes
						any_scope_pop = {
							pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
							total_size >= 1000
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# more likely if bankrupt
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						in_default = yes
						has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# Less likely in council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# more likely if angry non-unions
		if = {
			limit = {
				ig_approval <= -5
				NOT = { is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions }
			}
			subtract = {
				value = ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# less likely if content without ethnostate or Corporate State
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_ethnostate
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
					}
				}
				ig_approval >= 5
			}
			subtract = {
				value = ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# more likely for PB and armed forces
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_armed_forces
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# less likely for unions and intelligentsia
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		# more likely if in government with ethnostate or Corporate State
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_ethnostate
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
					}
					NOR = {
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_multicultural
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_national_supremacy
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_racial_segregation
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_cultural_exclusion
					}
				}
				is_in_government = yes
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the conservatives.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_conservative_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# red scare can make you more fascist
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = fascist_uptick
			}
			multiply = 1.5
		}
		# Fascism JE causes an uptick in fascism
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_journal_entry = je_fascism_1
						has_variable = completed_fascism_1_var
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 1.25
		}
		if = { #Brazil has Integralists instead
			limit = {
				owner = {
					c:BRZ ?= this
				}
			}
			multiply = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
		# Minority cultures won't favor highly ethno-supremacist ideologies
		if = {
			limit = {
				leader = {
					culture = {
						NOT = { is_primary_culture_of = prev.owner }
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# More likely if people are angry
		add = {
			value = owner.radical_fraction
			multiply = 100
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_fascist_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_fascist_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_fascist_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_fascist_favoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# More likely if paying war reparations
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_diplomatic_pact = {
						who = root.owner
						type = war_reparations
						is_initiator = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# More likely with a convenient scapegoat
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_incorporated = yes
						any_scope_pop = {
							pop_acceptance < acceptance_status_4
							total_size >= 1000
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# more likely if bankrupt
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						in_default = yes
						has_modifier = declared_bankruptcy
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# Less likely in council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# more likely if angry non-unions
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group.ig_approval <= -5
				NOT = { is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions }
			}
			add = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# less likely if content without ethnostate or Corporate State
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_ethnostate
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
					}
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval >= 5
			}
			subtract = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# more likely for PB and armed forces
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_armed_forces
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# less likely for unions and intelligentsia
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		# more likely if in government with ethnostate or Corporate State
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_ethnostate
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
					}
					NOR = {
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_multicultural
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_national_supremacy
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_racial_segregation
						is_enacting_law = law_type:law_cultural_exclusion
					}
				}
				interest_group = {
					is_in_government = yes
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the conservatives.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_conservative_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# red scare can make you more fascist
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = fascist_uptick
			}
			multiply = 1.5
		}
		# Fascism JE causes an uptick in fascism
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_journal_entry = je_fascism_1
						has_variable = completed_fascism_1_var
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 1.25
		}
		if = { #Brazil has Integralists instead
			limit = {
				owner = {
					c:BRZ ?= this
				}
			}
			multiply = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
					average_sol <= 10
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# More likely if in "government" under anarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anarchy
				}
				is_in_government = yes
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# Labour Association Laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_factory_councils
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_combination_acts
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_guild_system
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anti_strike_laws
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_right_to_associate
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_variable = election_anarchist_support }
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_variable = communism_1_done }
			}
			add = 100
		}
		# National Liberation Alliance
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = national_liberation_alliance_variable
					has_journal_entry = je_new_republic
				}
			}
			multiply = 1.10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# More likely if people are angry
		add = {
			value = owner.radical_fraction
			multiply = 100
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_anarchist_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_anarchist_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_anarchist_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_anarchist_favoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# More likely for angry IG's outside of council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval <= -5
			}
			subtract = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# More likely when SoL is low outside of council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
					average_sol <= 10
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# More likely if in "government" under anarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anarchy
				}
				is_in_government = yes
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# Labour Association Laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_factory_councils
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_combination_acts
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_guild_system
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_anti_strike_laws
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_right_to_associate
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

	character_ideology = yes

		law_regulated_augmentation_market = neutral
		law_mandatory_augmentation = strongly_approve
	}
	lawgroup_army_model = {
		law_mass_conscription = strongly_approve
		law_professional_army = approve
		law_national_militia = neutral
		law_peasant_levies = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_colonization = {
		law_neocolonialism = neutral
		law_no_colonial_affairs = neutral
		law_colonial_resettlement = approve
		law_frontier_colonization = approve
		law_colonial_exploitation = strongly_approve
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_jingoist_leader_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		# Agitators should have an ideology at odds with current laws
		NAND = {
			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mass_conscription
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_jingoist_leader_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mass_conscription
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# more likely if there's something to colonize nearby
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_decentralized_country = {
					has_overlapping_interests = ROOT.owner
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# more likely if you border a rival
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_rival_country = {
						any_neighbouring_state = {
							owner = root.owner
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# more likely if you're the defender in a war
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_at_war = yes
					any_scope_war = {
						defender_warleader = { this = ROOT.owner }
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# less likely for conservative French IG's
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					exists = c:FRA
					c:FRA ?= THIS
					has_journal_entry = je_divided_monarchists
				}
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the conservatives.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_conservative_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# More likely under Alexei II
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_character = {
						has_template = RUS_alexei_ii
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mass_conscription
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# more likely if there's something to colonize nearby
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					is_country_type = decentralized
					has_overlapping_interests = ROOT.owner
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# more likely if you border a rival
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_rival_country = {
						any_neighbouring_state = {
							owner = root.owner
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# more likely if you're the defender in a war
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_at_war = yes
					any_scope_war = {
						defender_warleader = { this = ROOT.owner }
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# less likely for conservative French IG's
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					exists = c:FRA
					c:FRA ?= THIS
					has_journal_entry = je_divided_monarchists
				}
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# More likely under Alexei II
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_character = {
						has_template = RUS_alexei_ii
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

			}

			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_resettlement
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_peasant_levies
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mass_conscription
					}
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		# more likely if a war you started isn't going well
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_at_war = yes
					any_scope_war = {
						attacker_warleader = { this = ROOT.owner }
						has_war_support = {
							target = root.owner
							value < 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 100
		}
		# more likely with devastation in incorporated states
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_incorporated = yes
						devastation > 0.2
					}
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Hungarian Revolution was successful.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hungarian_revolution_increased_liberalism
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 50
		# emerges to counter powerful armed forces
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					exists = ig:ig_armed_forces
					ig:ig_armed_forces ?= {
						is_powerful = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_resettlement
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_colonial_exploitation
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_peasant_levies
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mass_conscription
					}
				}
			}
			add = -25
		}
		# more likely if a war you started isn't going well
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_at_war = yes
					any_scope_war = {
						attacker_warleader = { this = ROOT.owner }
						has_war_support = {
							target = root.owner
							value < 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = 100
		}
		# more likely with devastation in incorporated states
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_scope_state = {
						is_incorporated = yes
						devastation > 0.2
					}
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				has_variable = spa_liberal_military_var
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = { # Fewer pacifist generals/admirals
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Hungarian Revolution was successful.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hungarian_revolution_increased_liberalism
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# more likely for intelligentsia
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant - greater bonus to this than usual
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_humanitarian_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_humanitarian_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 16
			}
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				has_variable = spa_liberal_military_var
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_humanitarian_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_humanitarian_favoured_laws
				multiply = 8
			}
		}
		# less likely for angry trade unions outside of Council Republic, they should go communist instead
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology_researched = socialism
					NOT = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic
					}
				}
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				interest_group.ig_approval < 5
			}
			add = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.5
		}
	}

							has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy

# Forced REPLACE due to existing section(s): lawgroup_governance_principles, lawgroup_distribution_of_power
REPLACE:ideology_orleanist = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/ideology_icons/ideology_leader/ideology_leader_orleanist.dds"
	character_ideology = yes
	lawgroup_inheritance = {
		law_primogeniture = disapprove
		law_partible = approve
		law_equal_inheritance = approve
		law_non_inheritable_usage_rights = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_governance_principles = {
		law_direct_democracy = disapprove
		law_corporation_state = disapprove
		law_monarchy = strongly_approve
		law_presidential_republic = neutral
		law_parliamentary_republic = disapprove
		law_corporate_state = neutral
		law_theocracy = disapprove
		law_council_republic = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_distribution_of_power = {
		law_algorithmic_governance = disapprove
		law_autocracy = disapprove
		law_oligarchy = neutral
		law_landed_voting = approve
		law_wealth_voting = approve
		law_census_voting = neutral
		law_universal_suffrage = disapprove
		law_anarchy = strongly_disapprove
		law_single_party_state = disapprove
		law_technocracy = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_economic_system = {
		law_laissez_faire = strongly_approve
		law_interventionism = neutral
		law_agrarianism = disapprove
		law_traditionalism = disapprove
		law_cooperative_ownership = strongly_disapprove
		law_command_economy = strongly_disapprove
		law_industry_banned = strongly_disapprove
		law_extraction_economy = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_trade_policy = {
		law_free_trade = strongly_approve
		law_mercantilism = disapprove
		law_protectionism = disapprove
		law_isolationism = strongly_disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_labour_associations = {
		law_combination_acts = approve
		law_guild_system = disapprove
		law_anti_strike_laws = neutral
		law_corporatized_unions = neutral
		law_right_to_associate = disapprove
		law_factory_councils = strongly_disapprove
	}
	country_trigger = {
		exists = c:FRA
		OR = {
			c:FRA = this
			civil_war_origin_country ?= c:FRA
		}
		NOR = {
			any_interest_group = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_paternalistic
			}
			has_variable = monarchy_stamped_out_var
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = legitimist_restoration_var
					has_variable = bonapartist_restoration_var
				}
				has_variable = one_true_french_dynasty
			}
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_orleanist_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		NOT = { has_role = agitator }
		ideology_orleanist_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 200
		# less likely in a theocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# less likely if IG is happy in a republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
				}
				ig_approval > 0
			}
			add = -100
		}
		# more likely for intelligentsia, industrialists, and PB with traditional economic laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
					is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
				}
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_agrarianism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_traditionalism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_isolationism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mercantilism
					}
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# more likely if the IG is unhappy with the monarchy, and that monarchy is not Orleanist
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
					NOT = { has_variable = orleanist_restoration_var }
				}
				ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# reduced unhappy modifier if it's not a monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
					NOT = { has_variable = orleanist_restoration_var }
				}
				ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 200
		# less likely in a theocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# less likely if IG is happy in a republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval > 0
			}
			add = -100
		}
		# more likely for intelligentsia, industrialists, and PB with traditional economic laws
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
					is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
					is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
				}
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_agrarianism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_traditionalism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_isolationism
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_mercantilism
					}
				}
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# more likely if the IG is unhappy with the monarchy, and that monarchy is not Orleanist
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
					NOT = { has_variable = orleanist_restoration_var }
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# reduced unhappy modifier if it's not a monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
					NOT = { has_variable = orleanist_restoration_var }
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 25
		}
		if = { # Orleanist agitators rare in Orleanist kingdoms
			limit = {
				has_role = agitator
				owner = {
					has_variable = orleanist_restoration_var
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

				has_role = agitator
				owner = {
					has_variable = bonapartist_restoration_var
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}

REPLACE:ideology_republican_leader = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/ideology_icons/ideology_leader/ideology_leader_republican.dds"
	character_ideology = yes
	lawgroup_inheritance = {
		law_primogeniture = disapprove
		law_partible = approve
		law_equal_inheritance = approve
		law_non_inheritable_usage_rights = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_governance_principles = {
		law_direct_democracy = neutral
		law_corporation_state = disapprove
		law_presidential_republic = strongly_approve
		law_parliamentary_republic = approve
		law_corporate_state = neutral
		law_council_republic = disapprove
		law_monarchy = disapprove
		law_theocracy = disapprove
	}
	lawgroup_bureaucracy = {
		law_elected_bureaucrats = approve
		law_appointed_bureaucrats = neutral
		law_hereditary_bureaucrats = disapprove
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_republican_leader_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		# Agitators should have an ideology at odds with current laws
		NAND = {
			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
				}
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_elected_bureaucrats
			}
		}
		# Monarchs cannot be republicans
		NAND = {
			owner = {
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
			OR = {
				is_ruler = yes
				is_heir = yes
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_republican_leader_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_republican_leader_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_republican_leader_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 25
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_republican_leader_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_republican_leader_favoured_laws
				multiply = 25
			}
		}
		# more likely if the IG is unhappy with the monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				}
				ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Hungarian Revolution was successful.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = hungarian_revolution_increased_liberalism
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Pedro JE victory
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = brz_enduring_empire
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# 1848
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
					OR = {
						capital.region = sr:region_north_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_south_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_england
						capital.region = sr:region_iberia
						capital.region = sr:region_france
						capital.region = sr:region_occitania
						capital.region = sr:region_rhine
						capital.region = sr:region_italy
						capital.region = sr:region_poland
						capital.region = sr:region_danubia
						capital.region = sr:region_balkans
						capital.region = sr:region_baltic
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = {
				value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = post_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_modifier = counter_revolutionary_fervor }
			}
			multiply = { value = 0.5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_republican_leader_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_republican_leader_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 25
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_republican_leader_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_republican_leader_favoured_laws
				multiply = 25
			}
		}
		# more likely if the IG is unhappy with the monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval < 0
			}
			add = 75
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}

			}
			add = 50
		}
		# 1848
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
					OR = {
						capital.region = sr:region_north_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_south_germany
						capital.region = sr:region_england
						capital.region = sr:region_iberia
						capital.region = sr:region_france
						capital.region = sr:region_occitania
						capital.region = sr:region_rhine
						capital.region = sr:region_italy
						capital.region = sr:region_poland
						capital.region = sr:region_danubia
						capital.region = sr:region_balkans
						capital.region = sr:region_baltic
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = {
				value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			}
			multiply = { value = 1.5 }
		}
		if = {

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/ideology_icons/ideology_leader/ideology_leader_royalist.dds"
	character_ideology = yes
	lawgroup_governance_principles = {
		law_direct_democracy = disapprove
		law_corporation_state = disapprove
		law_monarchy = strongly_approve
		law_presidential_republic = neutral
		law_parliamentary_republic = disapprove
		law_corporate_state = neutral
		law_theocracy = disapprove
		law_council_republic = strongly_disapprove
	}
	country_trigger = {
		# no monarchists in countries with strong republican tradition
		# no generic monarchists in France
		NOR = {
			c:FRA ?= this
			AND = {
				any_interest_group = {
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_paternalistic
				}
				NOT = {
					has_variable = brz_enduring_empire
				}
			}
			has_variable = monarchy_stamped_out_var
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		ideology_royalist_valid_trigger = yes
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_trigger = {
		# Agitators should have an ideology at odds with current laws

			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_royalist_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# less likely in a theocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# less likely if IG is happy in a republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
				}
				ig_approval > 0
			}
			add = -100
		}
		# more likely if IG is happy in a monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				}
				ig_approval > 5
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = brz_enduring_empire
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the conservatives.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_conservative_victory
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# less likely in a theocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# less likely if IG is happy in a republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy }
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval > 0
			}
			add = -100
		}
		# more likely if IG is happy in a monarchy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval > 5
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					OR = {

						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}

		}
	}

		law_hereditary_bureaucrats = strongly_disapprove
	}

		has_global_variable = positivism_invented
	}

		ideology_positivist_valid_trigger = yes
	}

		# Agitators should have an ideology at odds with current laws

			has_role = agitator
			owner = {
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_appointed_bureaucrats
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_technocracy
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_state_atheism
				has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_presidential_republic
			}
		}
		# Monarchs cannot be republicans
		NAND = {
			owner = {
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
			OR = {
				is_ruler = yes
				is_heir = yes
			}
		}
		interest_group = {
			ideology_positivist_valid_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	interest_group_leader_weight = {
		if = { # Baseline more likely if Catholic or ex-Catholic
			limit = {
				owner = {
				OR = {
					country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
						country_definition.religion = rel:catholic
					}
				}
			}
			value = 100
		}
		else = {
			value = 50
		}
		# More likely among angry IGs outside of a technocracy
		if = {
			limit = {

					NOT = {

					}

				multiply = 5

				value = owner.ideology_positivist_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 12
			}
		}
		# More likely in constitutional monarchies
		if = {
			limit = {

						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_census_voting
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_universal_suffrage

					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}

				owner = {

				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_variable = positivist_leaders_je_var
				}
			}
			add = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = positivist_leaders_increase_var
			}
			add = 75
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = positivist_leaders_large_increase_var
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = positivist_leaders_reward_var
			}
			add = 250
		}
		if = {

					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = rel:catholic
					owner.country_definition.religion = rel:catholic
				}
			}
			value = 100
		}

		}
		# More likely among angry IGs outside of a technocracy

		}
		# Modified directly by IG approval in a technocracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_technocracy
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_positivist_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_positivist_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 12
			}
		}
		# More likely in constitutional monarchies
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_wealth_voting
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_census_voting
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_landed_voting
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# More likely if Latin military commander
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = {
					OR = {
						has_discrimination_trait = language_hispanophone
						has_discrimination_trait = language_lusophone
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_role = admiral
					has_role = general
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}

				owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_favoured_laws
				multiply = 10
			}
		}
		# Modified directly by IG approval in a corporate state
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# less likely for landowners
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# less likely for devout due to their IG ideology
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# more likely for content trade unions and rural folk outside of council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
				}
				ig_approval >= 0
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_state_atheism }
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# corporatist boosts
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = corporatist_leaders_boost
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Corporatised Unions
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Ständestaat JE
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_journal_entry = je_standestaat
				}
			}
			add = 100
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Anti-Dreyfusards won
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = anti_dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# conservative and/or reactionary leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the conservatives.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_conservative_victory
			}
			add = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# More likely if issues are relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_disfavoured_laws > 0
			}
			add = {
				value = owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_disfavoured_laws
				multiply = 10
			}
		}
		# Less likely if issues are not relevant
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_favoured_laws > 0
			}
			subtract = {
				value = owner.ideology_corporatist_leader_favoured_laws
				multiply = 10
			}
		}
		# Modified directly by IG approval in a corporate state
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporate_state
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# less likely for landowners
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# less likely for devout due to their IG ideology
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_devout
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# more likely for content trade unions and rural folk outside of council republic
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
					is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
				}
				interest_group.ig_approval >= 0
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_council_republic }
					NOT = { has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_state_atheism }
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# Corporatised Unions
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
				owner = {
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_corporatized_unions
				}
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# Ständestaat JE
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_journal_entry = je_standestaat
				}
			}
			add = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism

				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# Angry IGs will try to oppose others' dictatorships
		if = {
			limit = {
				ig_approval <= -5
				NOR = {
					is_in_government = yes
					any_scope_character = {
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
			subtract = {
				value = ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# More common in republics
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		else = {
			add = -50
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if the Dreyfusards won.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dreyfusard_victory
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = spa_two_spains_liberal_victory
			}
			add = 25
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you succeed in Portugal's Second Liberalism.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = por_second_liberalism_victory
			}
			add = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = communist_ig_var
					has_variable = chose_vanguardism
					has_variable = chose_anarchism
					has_variable = chose_communism
					has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
					has_variable = chose_conservatism
					has_variable = chose_fascism
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
	non_interest_group_leader_weight = {
		value = 100
		# not very relevant if issues are already addressed
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_census_voting
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_wealth_voting
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_landed_voting
					}
					has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_elected_bureaucrats
				}
			}
			add = -50
		}
		# IGs will not sabotage their own dictatorships
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_autocracy
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_oligarchy
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_technocracy
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_single_party_state
					}
				}
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						is_in_government = yes
						any_scope_character = {
							is_ruler = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add = -75
		}
		# Angry IGs will try to oppose others' dictatorships
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					ig_approval <= -5
					NOR = {
						is_in_government = yes
						any_scope_character = {
							is_ruler = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			subtract = {
				value = interest_group.ig_approval
				multiply = 5
			}
		}
		# liberal and/or radical leaders have a higher spawn chance if you win the Two Spains as the liberals and choose to have woke commanders.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_role = general
					has_role = admiral
				}
				has_variable = spa_liberal_military_var
			}
			add = 50
		}
		# More common in republics
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
						has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
					}
				}
			}
			add = 25
		}
		else = {
			add = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				interest_group = {
					OR = {
						has_variable = communist_ig_var
						has_variable = chose_vanguardism
						has_variable = chose_anarchism
						has_variable = chose_communism
						has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
						has_variable = chose_conservatism
						has_variable = chose_fascism
					}
				}
			}
			multiply = 0.1
		}
	}
}
